Code and Data**: SQL code (raw_query) and parameters (params) are kept completely separate throughout execution\\n2. **No String Interpolation**: Django never uses string formatting (%), concatenation, or f-strings to insert parameters into SQL\\n3. **Database Driver Escaping**: Parameters are passed to cursor.execute(sql, params) where the database driver's native parameter binding mechanism escapes them\\n4. **Type-Safe Adaptation**: Parameter types are adapted to database-specific formats without modifying SQL\\n\\nWhen users follow Django's API correctly:\\n```python\\nAuthor.objects.raw(\\\"SELECT * FROM author WHERE name = %s\\\", [user_input])\\n```\\n\\nThe SQL template remains untouched, and user_input is escaped by the database driver,
